Notes:
A. The reported data does not comprise all signatory member brand/ retailers of the Accord and data will be added as they report. Two values that adjust with member data are the "Approximate Total number of Factories: 1613" and the "Approximate Total number of workers: 2,017,248"
B. Duplicate entries with same factory name and address have been removed. However, entries with same factory name but different addresses have been kept as reported.
C. The addresses of factories are as reported.
D. In the number of buildings column the 's' stands for 'sheds' -- generally meant to describe support function rooms/buildings inside factory premise. Generally one storied with no concrete roofs.
E. The "Number of stories of each building" and "Floors of the building which the factory occupies" columns contain values like "1/5; 2/1; 3/1;" This means building one has 5 stories, building 2 has 1 story and building 3 has 1 story.
F. At the time of this report the Accord members of record for factory information have reported Tier data for 1613 factories, shown in columns "Tier 1 or Tier 2 Factory" and "Tier 3 Factory."
